## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Component as VinHistoricalDataTable
    participant Effect as useEffect
    participant Redux as Redux Store
    participant Formatter as DiagnosticDataFormatter
    participant Table as BaseTable
    
    Component->>Effect: Mount/Props Change
    Effect->>Redux: fetchHistoricalData(solutionId, entityId, qualifier, dealerOrgId)
    Component->>Redux: useSelector(getHistoryByQualifier)
    Redux-->>Component: history data
    Component->>Formatter: getDiagonsticLabel(qualifier)
    Formatter-->>Component: label
    Component->>Formatter: getColorByState(state)
    Formatter-->>Component: color
    Component->>Component: map historicalData to formattedData
    Component->>Table: render with formattedData and columns
    Table-->>Component: rendered table
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Mounting
    Mounting --> FetchingData: useEffect triggered
    FetchingData --> Loading: fetchHistoricalData called
    Loading --> DataReceived: Redux store updated
    DataReceived --> FormattingData: Format with getDiagonsticLabel & getColorByState
    FormattingData --> Rendering: Pass to BaseTable
    Rendering --> [*]
    DataReceived --> FetchingData: Props change
```
